| serverlessComputeSettings       | Settings for serverless compute created in the workspace                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | [ServerlessComputeSettings_STATUS](#ServerlessComputeSettings_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                       |
| serviceManagedResourcesSettings | The service managed resource settings.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | [ServiceManagedResourcesSettings_STATUS](#ServiceManagedResourcesSettings_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                           |
| serviceProvisionedResourceGroup | The name of the managed resource group created by workspace RP in customer subscription if the workspace is CMK workspace                                                                                                                                                                                                 | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                      |
| sharedPrivateLinkResources      | The list of shared private link resources in this workspace.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              | [SharedPrivateLinkResource_STATUS[]](#SharedPrivateLinkResource_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                     |
| sku                             | The sku of the workspace.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | [Sku_STATUS](#Sku_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                   |
| storageAccount                  | ARM id of the storage account associated with this workspace. This cannot be changed once the workspace has been created                                                                                                                                                                                                  | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                      |
| storageHnsEnabled               | If the storage associated with the workspace has hierarchical namespace(HNS) enabled.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                        |
| systemData                      | Azure Resource Manager metadata containing createdBy and modifiedBy information.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | [SystemData_STATUS](#SystemData_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                     |
| tags                            | Contains resource tags defined as key/value pairs.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | map[string]string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                           |
| tenantId                        | The tenant id associated with this workspace.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                      |
| type                            | The type of the resource. E.g. "Microsoft.Compute/virtualMachines" or "Microsoft.Storage/storageAccounts"                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                      |
| v1LegacyMode                    | Enabling v1_legacy_mode may prevent you from using features provided by the v2 API.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                        |
| workspaceHubConfig              | WorkspaceHub's configuration object.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | [WorkspaceHubConfig_STATUS](#WorkspaceHubConfig_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                     |
| workspaceId                     | The immutable id associated with this workspace.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                      |

| serverlessComputeCustomSubnetReference | The resource ID of an existing virtual network subnet in which serverless compute nodes should be deployed                                     | [genruntime.ResourceReference](https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#ResourceReference)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| serverlessComputeNoPublicIP            | The flag to signal if serverless compute nodes deployed in custom vNet would have no public IP addresses for a workspace with private endpoint | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                           |

Sku{#Sku}
---------

The resource model definition representing SKU

Used by: [Registry_Spec](#Registry_Spec), [Workspace_Spec](#Workspace_Spec), and [WorkspacesCompute_Spec](#WorkspacesCompute_Spec).

| Property | Description                                                                                                                                          | Type                                            |
|----------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------|
| capacity | If the SKU supports scale out/in then the capacity integer should be included. If scale out/in is not possible for the resource this may be omitted. | int<br/><small>Optional</small>                 |
| family   | If the service has different generations of hardware, for the same SKU, then that can be captured here.                                              | string<br/><small>Optional</small>              |
| name     | The name of the SKU. Ex - P3. It is typically a letter+number code                                                                                   | string<br/><small>Required</small>              |
| size     | The SKU size. When the name field is the combination of tier and some other value, this would be the standalone code.                                | string<br/><small>Optional</small>              |
| tier     | This field is required to be implemented by the Resource Provider if the service has more than one tier, but is not required on a PUT.               | [SkuTier](#SkuTier)<br/><small>Optional</small> |

Sku_STATUS{#Sku_STATUS}
-----------------------

The resource model definition representing SKU

Used by: [RegistryTrackedResource_STATUS](#RegistryTrackedResource_STATUS), [Workspace_STATUS](#Workspace_STATUS), and [WorkspacesCompute_STATUS](#WorkspacesCompute_STATUS).

| Property | Description                                                                                                                                          | Type                                                          |
|----------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------|
| capacity | If the SKU supports scale out/in then the capacity integer should be included. If scale out/in is not possible for the resource this may be omitted. | int<br/><small>Optional</small>                               |
| family   | If the service has different generations of hardware, for the same SKU, then that can be captured here.                                              | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                            |
| name     | The name of the SKU. Ex - P3. It is typically a letter+number code                                                                                   | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                            |
| size     | The SKU size. When the name field is the combination of tier and some other value, this would be the standalone code.                                | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                            |
| tier     | This field is required to be implemented by the Resource Provider if the service has more than one tier, but is not required on a PUT.               | [SkuTier_STATUS](#SkuTier_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small> |

| description        | The description of the Machine Learning compute.                                                                                              | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                        |
| disableLocalAuth   | Opt-out of local authentication and ensure customers can use only MSI and AAD exclusively for authentication.                                 | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                          |
| isAttachedCompute  | Indicating whether the compute was provisioned by user and brought from outside if true, or machine learning service provisioned it if false. | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                          |
| modifiedOn         | The time at which the compute was last modified.                                                                                              | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                        |
| properties         | AKS properties                                                                                                                                | [AKS_Properties_STATUS](#AKS_Properties_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>               |
| provisioningErrors | Errors during provisioning                                                                                                                    | [ErrorResponse_STATUS[]](#ErrorResponse_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>               |
| provisioningState  | The provision state of the cluster. Valid values are Unknown, Updating, Provisioning, Succeeded, and Failed.                                  | [AKS_ProvisioningState_STATUS](#AKS_ProvisioningState_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| resourceId         | ARM resource id of the underlying compute                                                                                                     | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                        |

| isAttachedCompute  | Indicating whether the compute was provisioned by user and brought from outside if true, or machine learning service provisioned it if false. | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                      |
| modifiedOn         | The time at which the compute was last modified.                                                                                              | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                    |
| properties         | HDInsight compute properties                                                                                                                  | [HDInsightProperties_STATUS](#HDInsightProperties_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                 |
| provisioningErrors | Errors during provisioning                                                                                                                    | [ErrorResponse_STATUS[]](#ErrorResponse_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                           |
| provisioningState  | The provision state of the cluster. Valid values are Unknown, Updating, Provisioning, Succeeded, and Failed.                                  | [HDInsight_ProvisioningState_STATUS](#HDInsight_ProvisioningState_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| resourceId         | ARM resource id of the underlying compute                                                                                                     | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                    |

|-----------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| enableNodePublicIp          | Enable or disable node public IP address provisioning. Possible values are: Possible values are: true - Indicates that the compute nodes will have public IPs provisioned. false - Indicates that the compute nodes will have a private endpoint and no public IPs.                                                                                                                                                                                                             | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                  |
| isolatedNetwork             | Network is isolated or not                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                  |
| osType                      | Compute OS Type                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | [AmlComputeProperties_OsType](#AmlComputeProperties_OsType)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                           |
| propertyBag                 | A property bag containing additional properties.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | map[string]v1.JSON<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                    |
| remoteLoginPortPublicAccess | State of the public SSH port. Possible values are: Disabled - Indicates that the public ssh port is closed on all nodes of the cluster. Enabled - Indicates that the public ssh port is open on all nodes of the cluster. NotSpecified - Indicates that the public ssh port is closed on all nodes of the cluster if VNet is defined, else is open all public nodes. It can be default only during cluster creation time, after creation it will be either enabled or disabled. | [AmlComputeProperties_RemoteLoginPortPublicAccess](#AmlComputeProperties_RemoteLoginPortPublicAccess)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| scaleSettings               | Scale settings for AML Compute                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | [ScaleSettings](#ScaleSettings)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                       |
| subnet                      | Virtual network subnet resource ID the compute nodes belong to.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | [ResourceId](#ResourceId)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                             |
| userAccountCredentials      | Credentials for an administrator user account that will be created on each compute node.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | [UserAccountCredentials](#UserAccountCredentials)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                     |
| virtualMachineImage         | Virtual Machine image for AML Compute - windows only                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | [VirtualMachineImage](#VirtualMachineImage)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                           |
| vmPriority                  | Virtual Machine priority                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | [AmlComputeProperties_VmPriority](#AmlComputeProperties_VmPriority)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                   |
| vmSize                      | Virtual Machine Size                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                |

AmlComputeProperties_STATUS{#AmlComputeProperties_STATUS}
---------------------------------------------------------

AML Compute properties

Used by: [AmlCompute_STATUS](#AmlCompute_STATUS).

| Property                      | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Type                                                                                                                                            |
|-------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| allocationState               | Allocation state of the compute. Possible values are: steady - Indicates that the compute is not resizing. There are no changes to the number of compute nodes in the compute in progress. A compute enters this state when it is created and when no operations are being performed on the compute to change the number of compute nodes. resizing - Indicates that the compute is resizing; that is, compute nodes are being added to or removed from the compute.            | [AmlComputeProperties_AllocationState_STATUS](#AmlComputeProperties_AllocationState_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                         |
| allocationStateTransitionTime | The time at which the compute entered its current allocation state.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                              |
| currentNodeCount              | The number of compute nodes currently assigned to the compute.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | int<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                 |
| enableNodePublicIp            | Enable or disable node public IP address provisioning. Possible values are: Possible values are: true - Indicates that the compute nodes will have public IPs provisioned. false - Indicates that the compute nodes will have a private endpoint and no public IPs.                                                                                                                                                                                                             | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                |
| errors                        | Collection of errors encountered by various compute nodes during node setup.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    | [ErrorResponse_STATUS[]](#ErrorResponse_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                     |
| isolatedNetwork               | Network is isolated or not                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                |
| nodeStateCounts               | Counts of various node states on the compute.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | [NodeStateCounts_STATUS](#NodeStateCounts_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                   |
| osType                        | Compute OS Type                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | [AmlComputeProperties_OsType_STATUS](#AmlComputeProperties_OsType_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                           |
| propertyBag                   | A property bag containing additional properties.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | map[string]v1.JSON<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                  |
| remoteLoginPortPublicAccess   | State of the public SSH port. Possible values are: Disabled - Indicates that the public ssh port is closed on all nodes of the cluster. Enabled - Indicates that the public ssh port is open on all nodes of the cluster. NotSpecified - Indicates that the public ssh port is closed on all nodes of the cluster if VNet is defined, else is open all public nodes. It can be default only during cluster creation time, after creation it will be either enabled or disabled. | [AmlComputeProperties_RemoteLoginPortPublicAccess_STATUS](#AmlComputeProperties_RemoteLoginPortPublicAccess_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| scaleSettings                 | Scale settings for AML Compute                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | [ScaleSettings_STATUS](#ScaleSettings_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                       |
| subnet                        | Virtual network subnet resource ID the compute nodes belong to.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 | [ResourceId_STATUS](#ResourceId_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                             |
| targetNodeCount               | The target number of compute nodes for the compute. If the allocationState is resizing, this property denotes the target node count for the ongoing resize operation. If the allocationState is steady, this property denotes the target node count for the previous resize operation.                                                                                                                                                                                          | int<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                 |
| userAccountCredentials        | Credentials for an administrator user account that will be created on each compute node.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | [UserAccountCredentials_STATUS](#UserAccountCredentials_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                     |
| virtualMachineImage           | Virtual Machine image for AML Compute - windows only                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | [VirtualMachineImage_STATUS](#VirtualMachineImage_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                           |
| vmPriority                    | Virtual Machine priority                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | [AmlComputeProperties_VmPriority_STATUS](#AmlComputeProperties_VmPriority_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                   |
| vmSize                        | Virtual Machine Size                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                              |

CustomKeys{#CustomKeys}

| nodeSize            | Node size.                                                     | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                    |

| poolName            | Pool name.                                                     | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                    |
| resourceGroup       | Name of the resource group in which workspace is located.      | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                    |
| sparkVersion        | Spark version.                                                 | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                    |
| subscriptionId      | Azure subscription identifier.                                 | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                    |
| workspaceName       | Name of Azure Machine Learning workspace.                      | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                    |

WorkspaceConnectionOAuth2{#WorkspaceConnectionOAuth2}
-----------------------------------------------------

ClientId and ClientSecret are required. Other properties are optional depending on each OAuth2 provider's implementation.

Used by: [OAuth2AuthTypeWorkspaceConnectionProperties](#OAuth2AuthTypeWorkspaceConnectionProperties).

| Property           | Description                                                                                                                     | Type                                                                                                                                                         |
|--------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| authUrl            | Required by Concur connection category                                                                                          | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                           |
| clientId           | Client id in the format of UUID                                                                                                 | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                           |
| clientIdFromConfig | Client id in the format of UUID                                                                                                 | [genruntime.ConfigMapReference](https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#ConfigMapReference)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| clientSecret       |                                                                                                                                 | [genruntime.SecretReference](https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#SecretReference)<br/><small>Optional</small>       |
| developerToken     | Required by GoogleAdWords connection category                                                                                   | [genruntime.SecretReference](https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#SecretReference)<br/><small>Optional</small>       |
| password           |                                                                                                                                 | [genruntime.SecretReference](https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#SecretReference)<br/><small>Optional</small>       |
| refreshToken       | Required by GoogleBigQuery, GoogleAdWords, Hubspot, QuickBooks, Square, Xero, Zoho where user needs to get RefreshToken offline | [genruntime.SecretReference](https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#SecretReference)<br/><small>Optional</small>       |
| tenantId           | Required by QuickBooks and Xero connection categories                                                                           | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                           |
| tenantIdFromConfig | Required by QuickBooks and Xero connection categories                                                                           | [genruntime.ConfigMapReference](https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#ConfigMapReference)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| username           | Concur, ServiceNow auth server AccessToken grant type is `Password` which requires UsernamePassword                             | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                                                           |

WorkspaceConnectionOAuth2_STATUS{#WorkspaceConnectionOAuth2_STATUS}
-------------------------------------------------------------------

ClientId and ClientSecret are required. Other properties are optional depending on each OAuth2 provider's implementation.

Used by: [OAuth2AuthTypeWorkspaceConnectionProperties_STATUS](#OAuth2AuthTypeWorkspaceConnectionProperties_STATUS).

| Property | Description                                                                                         | Type                               |
|----------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------|
| authUrl  | Required by Concur connection category                                                              | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| clientId | Client id in the format of UUID                                                                     | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |

Use "ssh-keygen -t rsa -b 2048" to generate your SSH key pairs.                                                                                                                                  | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                                    |
| sshPublicAccess | State of the public SSH port. Possible values are: Disabled - Indicates that the public ssh port is closed on this instance. Enabled - Indicates that the public ssh port is open and accessible according to the VNet/subnet policy if applicable. | [ComputeInstanceSshSettings_SshPublicAccess](#ComputeInstanceSshSettings_SshPublicAccess)<br/><small>Optional</small> |

ComputeStartStopSchedule{#ComputeStartStopSchedule}
---------------------------------------------------

Compute start stop schedule properties

Used by: [ComputeSchedules](#ComputeSchedules).

| Property    | Description                            | Type                                                                  |
|-------------|----------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------|
| action      | [Required] The compute power action.   | [ComputePowerAction](#ComputePowerAction)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| cron        | Required if triggerType is Cron.       | [Cron](#Cron)<br/><small>Optional</small>                             |
| recurrence  | Required if triggerType is Recurrence. | [Recurrence](#Recurrence)<br/><small>Optional</small>                 |
| schedule    | [Deprecated] Not used any more.        | [ScheduleBase](#ScheduleBase)<br/><small>Optional</small>             |
| status      | Is the schedule enabled or disabled?   | [ScheduleStatus](#ScheduleStatus)<br/><small>Optional</small>         |
| triggerType | [Required] The schedule trigger type.  | [ComputeTriggerType](#ComputeTriggerType)<br/><small>Optional</small> |

|--------------------|-------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| action             | [Required] The compute power action.      | [ComputePowerAction_STATUS](#ComputePowerAction_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                   |

| provisioningStatus | The current deployment state of schedule. | [ComputeStartStopSchedule_ProvisioningStatus_STATUS](#ComputeStartStopSchedule_ProvisioningStatus_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| recurrence         | Required if triggerType is Recurrence.    | [Recurrence_STATUS](#Recurrence_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                   |
| schedule           | [Deprecated] Not used any more.           | [ScheduleBase_STATUS](#ScheduleBase_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                               |
| status             | Is the schedule enabled or disabled?      | [ScheduleStatus_STATUS](#ScheduleStatus_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                           |

VolumeDefinition{#VolumeDefinition}
-----------------------------------

Describes the volume configuration for the container

Used by: [CustomService](#CustomService).

| Property    | Description                                                                    | Type                                                                        |
|-------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| bind        | Bind Options of the mount                                                      | [BindOptions](#BindOptions)<br/><small>Optional</small>                     |
| consistency | Consistency of the volume                                                      | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                          |
| readOnly    | Indicate whether to mount volume as readOnly. Default value for this is false. | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                            |
| source      | Source of the mount. For bind mounts this is the host path.                    | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                          |
| target      | Target of the mount. For bind mounts this is the path in the container.        | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                          |
| tmpfs       | tmpfs option of the mount                                                      | [TmpfsOptions](#TmpfsOptions)<br/><small>Optional</small>                   |
| type        | Type of Volume Definition. Possible Values: bind,volume,tmpfs,npipe            | [VolumeDefinition_Type](#VolumeDefinition_Type)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| volume      | Volume Options of the mount                                                    | [VolumeOptions](#VolumeOptions)<br/><small>Optional</small>                 |

| readOnly    | Indicate whether to mount volume as readOnly. Default value for this is false. | bool<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                          |
| source      | Source of the mount. For bind mounts this is the host path.                    | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                        |
| target      | Target of the mount. For bind mounts this is the path in the container.        | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                        |
| tmpfs       | tmpfs option of the mount                                                      | [TmpfsOptions_STATUS](#TmpfsOptions_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                   |
| type        | Type of Volume Definition. Possible Values: bind,volume,tmpfs,npipe            | [VolumeDefinition_Type_STATUS](#VolumeDefinition_Type_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small> |

Cron{#Cron}
-----------

The workflow trigger cron for ComputeStartStop schedule type.

Used by: [ComputeStartStopSchedule](#ComputeStartStopSchedule).

| Property   | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Type                               |
|------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------|
| expression | [Required] Specifies cron expression of schedule. The expression should follow NCronTab format.                                                                                                                  | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| startTime  | The start time in yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss format.                                                                                                                                                                    | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| timeZone   | Specifies time zone in which the schedule runs. TimeZone should follow Windows time zone format. Refer: https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/windows-hardware/manufacture/desktop/default-time-zones?view=windows-11 | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |

Used by: [ComputeStartStopSchedule_STATUS](#ComputeStartStopSchedule_STATUS).

| Property   | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                      | Type                               |
|------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------|
| expression | [Required] Specifies cron expression of schedule. The expression should follow NCronTab format.                                                                                                                  | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| startTime  | The start time in yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss format.                                                                                                                                                                    | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| timeZone   | Specifies time zone in which the schedule runs. TimeZone should follow Windows time zone format. Refer: https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/windows-hardware/manufacture/desktop/default-time-zones?view=windows-11 | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |

| Property           | Description                               | Type                                                                                              |
|--------------------|-------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| id                 | A system assigned id for the schedule.    | string<br/><small>Optional</small>                                                                |
| provisioningStatus | The current deployment state of schedule. | [ScheduleProvisioningState_STATUS](#ScheduleProvisioningState_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| status             | Is the schedule enabled or disabled?      | [ScheduleStatus_STATUS](#ScheduleStatus_STATUS)<br/><small>Optional</small>                       |

ScheduleStatus{#ScheduleStatus}

Used by: [ComputeStartStopSchedule](#ComputeStartStopSchedule), and [ScheduleBase](#ScheduleBase).

| Value      | Description |
|------------|-------------|
| "Disabled" |             |
| "Enabled"  |             |

Used by: [ScriptsToExecute](#ScriptsToExecute), and [ScriptsToExecute](#ScriptsToExecute).

| Property        | Description                                                  | Type                               |

| scriptSource    | The storage source of the script: workspace.                 | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |
| timeout         | Optional time period passed to timeout command.              | string<br/><small>Optional</small> |
